à®-à®à¯ : agni: `It is derived from three verbs, says S@a#kapu#ni from going, from shining or burning, and from leading, He, indeed, takes the letter a from the root ( to go), the letter g from the root anj (to shine), dah (to burn), with  the root ni (to lead) as the last member. - (The Nighantu & the Nirukta, translated by Lakshman Sarup, p.120).
